2024-05-16 11:27:26.177 | ERROR    | metagpt.utils.common:log_it:554 - Finished call to 'MCTS.Lingma.ask_llm_location_file.ChatGPT.get_reward' after 73.340(s), this was the 1st time calling it. exp: no score found for The issue reported is related to the `django.utils.text.slugify()` function not stripping leading and trailing dashes and underscores from the resulting slug, which is contrary to the user's expectation. The user expects the output of `slugify("___This is a test ---")` to be `this-is-a-test` without any leading or trailing hyphens (dashes) or underscores. However, the current implementation keeps these characters.

From the provided issue description, we can see that there's a clear requirement for the function to remove leading and trailing underscores and hyphens. The code provided is a wrapper function `slugify(value)` in `django/template/defaultfilters.py` which calls `_slugify(value)` internally. As per the Django documentation, the expected behavior of `slugify` is to convert to ASCII, replace spaces with hyphens, to lowercase, remove unwanted characters, and also to strip leading and trailing whitespace.
